<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">for</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">(</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;i=</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">0</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;i&lt;count;&nbsp;i++){&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;list.add(<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;SmsSender());&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">测试类：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8194653">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8194653">copy</a>
</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Test&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;main(String[]&nbsp;args)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Builder&nbsp;builder&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Builder();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;builder.produceMailSender(<span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">10</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">从这点看出，建造者模式将很多功能集成到一个类里，这个类可以创造出比较复杂的东西。所以与工程模式的区别就是：工厂模式关注的是创建单个产品，而建造者模式则关注创建符合对象，多个部分。因此，是选择工厂模式还是建造者模式，依实际情况而定。</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><strong><span style="color: #006600;">5、原型模式（Prototype）</span></strong></p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">原型模式虽然是创建型的模式，但是与工程模式没有关系，从名字即可看出，该模式的思想就是将一个对象作为原型，对其进行复制、克隆，产生一个和原对象类似的新对象。本小结会通过对象的复制，进行讲解。在Java中，复制对象是通过clone()实现的，先创建一个原型类：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8194653">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8194653">copy</a>
</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Prototype&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">implements</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Cloneable&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Object&nbsp;clone()&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">throws</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;CloneNotSupportedException&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Prototype&nbsp;proto&nbsp;=&nbsp;(Prototype)&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">super</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">.clone();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">return</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;proto;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">很简单，一个原型类，只需要实现Cloneable接口，覆写clone方法，此处clone方法可以改成任意的名称，因为Cloneable接口是个空接口，你可以任意定义实现类的方法名，如cloneA或者cloneB，因为此处的重点是super.clone()这句话，super.clone()调用的是Object的clone()方法，而在Object类中，clone()是native的，具体怎么实现，我会在另一篇文章中，关于解读Java中本地方法的调用，此处不再深究。在这儿，我将结合对象的浅复制和深复制来说一下，首先需要了解对象深、浅复制的概念：</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">浅复制：将一个对象复制后，基本数据类型的变量都会重新创建，而引用类型，指向的还是原对象所指向的。</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">深复制：将一个对象复制后，不论是基本数据类型还有引用类型，都是重新创建的。简单来说，就是深复制进行了完全彻底的复制，而浅复制不彻底。</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">此处，写一个深浅复制的例子：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8194653">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8194653">copy</a>
</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Prototype&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">implements</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Cloneable,&nbsp;Serializable&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">final</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">long</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;serialVersionUID&nbsp;=&nbsp;1L;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;String&nbsp;string;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;SerializableObject&nbsp;obj;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*&nbsp;浅复制&nbsp;*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Object&nbsp;clone()&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">throws</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;CloneNotSupportedException&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Prototype&nbsp;proto&nbsp;=&nbsp;(Prototype)&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">super</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">.clone();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">return</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;proto;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*&nbsp;深复制&nbsp;*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Object&nbsp;deepClone()&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">throws</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;IOException,&nbsp;ClassNotFoundException&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ByteArrayOutputStream&nbsp;bos&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;ByteArrayOutputStream();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ObjectOutputStream&nbsp;oos&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;ObjectOutputStream(bos);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;oos.writeObject(<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">this</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*&nbsp;读出二进制流产生的新对象&nbsp;*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ByteArrayInputStream&nbsp;bis&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;ByteArrayInputStream(bos.toByteArray());&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ObjectInputStream&nbsp;ois&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;ObjectInputStream(bis);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">return</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;string;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">return</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;obj;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">this</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">.obj&nbsp;=&nbsp;obj;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;SerializableObject&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">implements</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Serializable&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">final</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">long</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;serialVersionUID&nbsp;=&nbsp;1L;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<div style="font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;</div>
<div style="font-size: 14px;">要实现深复制，需要采用流的形式读入当前对象的二进制输入，再写出二进制数据对应的对象。</div>
<div style="font-size: 14px;">
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">我们接着讨论设计模式，上篇文章我讲完了5种创建型模式，这章开始，我将讲下7种结构型模式：适配器模式、装饰模式、代理模式、外观模式、桥接模式、组合模式、享元模式。其中对象的适配器模式是各种模式的起源，我们看下面的图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1187/e28698b9-994e-3fa8-8810-16f30e7cf3e3.jpg" alt="" title="点击查看原始大小图片" class="magplus" width="700" height="371"></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;适配器模式将某个类的接口转换成客户端期望的另一个接口表示，目的是消除由于接口不匹配所造成的类的兼容性问题。主要分为三类：类的适配器模式、对象的适配器模式、接口的适配器模式。首先，我们来看看<strong><span style="color: #3333ff;">类的适配器模式</span></strong>，先看类图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1189/6b2d13aa-7cc7-3e98-9764-bdcb2c64f795.jpg" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">核心思想就是：有一个Source类，拥有一个方法，待适配，目标接口时Targetable，通过Adapter类，将Source的功能扩展到Targetable里，看代码：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">

</div>
</div>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;method1()&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">Adapter类继承Source类，实现Targetable接口，下面是测试类：</p>

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">this is original method!<br>this is the targetable method!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">这样Targetable接口的实现类就具有了Source类的功能。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><strong><span style="color: #3333ff;">对象的适配器模式</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">基本思路和类的适配器模式相同，只是将Adapter类作修改，这次不继承Source类，而是持有Source类的实例，以达到解决兼容性的问题。看图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1191/0aabe35b-5b79-3ead-838f-9d4b6fbd774d.jpg" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">只需要修改Adapter类的源码即可：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Source&nbsp;source;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Wrapper(Source&nbsp;source){&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">super</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">this</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">.source&nbsp;=&nbsp;source;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;method2()&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;System.out.println(<span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"this&nbsp;is&nbsp;the&nbsp;targetable&nbsp;method!"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #646464; padding: 0px;">@Override</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;method1()&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;source.method1();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">测试类：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">

</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;AdapterTest&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;main(String[]&nbsp;args)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Source&nbsp;source&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Source();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Targetable&nbsp;target&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Wrapper(source);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;target.method1();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;target.method2();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出与第一种一样，只是适配的方法不同而已。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">第三种适配器模式是<strong><span style="color: #3333ff;">接口的适配器模式</span></strong>，接口的适配器是这样的：有时我们写的一个接口中有多个抽象方法，当我们写该接口的实现类时，必须实现该接口的所有方法，这明显有时比较浪费，因为并不是所有的方法都是我们需要的，有时只需要某一些，此处为了解决这个问题，我们引入了接口的适配器模式，借助于一个抽象类，该抽象类实现了该接口，实现了所有的方法，而我们不和原始的接口打交道，只和该抽象类取得联系，所以我们写一个类，继承该抽象类，重写我们需要的方法就行。看一下类图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1193/a604fca8-e0c6-3e4e-b00a-49da21595b4e.jpg" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">这个很好理解，在实际开发中，我们也常会遇到这种接口中定义了太多的方法，以致于有时我们在一些实现类中并不是都需要。看代码：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">

</div>
</div>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;method1();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;method2();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">测试输出：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">the sourceable interface's first Sub1!<br>the sourceable interface's second Sub2!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">达到了我们的效果！</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;讲了这么多，总结一下三种适配器模式的应用场景：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">类的适配器模式：当希望将<strong><span style="color: #3333ff;">一个类</span></strong>转换成满足<strong><span style="color: #3333ff;">另一个新接口</span></strong>的类时，可以使用类的适配器模式，创建一个新类，继承原有的类，实现新的接口即可。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">对象的适配器模式：当希望将一个对象转换成满足另一个新接口的对象时，可以创建一个Wrapper类，持有原类的一个实例，在Wrapper类的方法中，调用实例的方法就行。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">接口的适配器模式：当不希望实现一个接口中所有的方法时，可以创建一个抽象类Wrapper，实现所有方法，我们写别的类的时候，继承抽象类即可。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><strong><span style="color: #006600;">7、装饰模式（Decorator）</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">顾名思义，装饰模式就是给一个对象增加一些新的功能，而且是动态的，要求装饰对象和被装饰对象实现同一个接口，装饰对象持有被装饰对象的实例，关系图如下：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1195/e1b8b6a3-0150-31ae-8f77-7c3d888b6f80.jpg" height="228" width="382" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">Source类是被装饰类，Decorator类是一个装饰类，可以为Source类动态的添加一些功能，代码如下：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;main(String[]&nbsp;args)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Sourceable&nbsp;source&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Source();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Sourceable&nbsp;obj&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Decorator(source);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;obj.method();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">before decorator!<br>the original method!<br>after decorator!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">装饰器模式的应用场景：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">1、需要扩展一个类的功能。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">2、动态的为一个对象增加功能，而且还能动态撤销。（继承不能做到这一点，继承的功能是静态的，不能动态增删。）</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">缺点：产生过多相似的对象，不易排错！</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>8、代理模式（Proxy）</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">其实每个模式名称就表明了该模式的作用，代理模式就是多一个代理类出来，替原对象进行一些操作，比如我们在租房子的时候回去找中介，为什么呢？因为你对该地区房屋的信息掌握的不够全面，希望找一个更熟悉的人去帮你做，此处的代理就是这个意思。再如我们有的时候打官司，我们需要请律师，因为律师在法律方面有专长，可以替我们进行操作，表达我们的想法。先来看看关系图：<img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1197/ea094ad9-efc5-337d-a8e8-ce9223511144.jpg" height="226" width="462" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">根据上文的阐述，代理模式就比较容易的理解了，我们看下代码：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8239539">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8239539">copy</a>
</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">interface</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Sourceable&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;method();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">before proxy!<br>the original method!<br>after proxy!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">代理模式的应用场景：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">如果已有的方法在使用的时候需要对原有的方法进行改进，此时有两种办法：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">1、修改原有的方法来适应。这样违反了“对扩展开放，对修改关闭”的原则。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">2、就是采用一个代理类调用原有的方法，且对产生的结果进行控制。这种方法就是代理模式。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">使用代理模式，可以将功能划分的更加清晰，有助于后期维护！</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><strong><span style="color: #006600;">9、外观模式（Facade）</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">外观模式是为了解决类与类之家的依赖关系的，像spring一样，可以将类和类之间的关系配置到配置文件中，而外观模式就是将他们的关系放在一个Facade类中，降低了类类之间的耦合度，该模式中没有涉及到接口，看下类图：（我们以一个计算机的启动过程为例）</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1199/eebe2103-6ced-35f2-8664-3a2e8a557f81.jpg" height="294" width="544" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">我们先看下实现类：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8239539">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8239539">copy</a>
</div>
</div>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cpu.startup();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;disk.startup();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cpu.shutdown();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;memory.shutdown();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;disk.shutdown();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;System.out.println(<span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"computer&nbsp;closed!"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">User类如下：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
