</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;User&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;main(String[]&nbsp;args)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Computer&nbsp;computer&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Computer();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;computer.startup();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;computer.shutdown();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">start the computer!<br>cpu startup!<br>memory startup!<br>disk startup!<br>start computer finished!<br>begin to close the computer!<br>cpu shutdown!<br>memory shutdown!<br>disk shutdown!<br>computer closed!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">如果我们没有Computer类，那么，CPU、Memory、Disk他们之间将会相互持有实例，产生关系，这样会造成严重的依赖，修改一个类，可能会带来其他类的修改，这不是我们想要看到的，有了Computer类，他们之间的关系被放在了Computer类里，这样就起到了解耦的作用，这，就是外观模式！</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>10、桥接模式（Bridge）</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">桥接模式就是把事物和其具体实现分开，使他们可以各自独立的变化。桥接的用意是：<strong><span style="color: #ff0000;">将抽象化与实现化解耦，使得二者可以独立变化</span></strong>，像我们常用的JDBC桥DriverManager一样，JDBC进行连接数据库的时候，在各个数据库之间进行切换，基本不需要动太多的代码，甚至丝毫不用动，原因就是JDBC提供统一接口，每个数据库提供各自的实现，用一个叫做数据库驱动的程序来桥接就行了。我们来看看关系图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1201/35f0b172-b976-3757-bb51-c65d5c9ce68e.jpg" height="247" width="640" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">实现代码：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">先定义接口：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8239539">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8239539">copy</a>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*调用第二个对象*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Sourceable&nbsp;source2&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;SourceSub2();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;bridge.setSource(source2);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;bridge.method();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">output：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">this is the first sub!<br>this is the second sub!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">这样，就通过对Bridge类的调用，实现了对接口Sourceable的实现类SourceSub1和SourceSub2的调用。接下来我再画个图，大家就应该明白了，因为这个图是我们JDBC连接的原理，有数据库学习基础的，一结合就都懂了。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1203/6f713d07-1409-3312-99c9-fa6b0909f0b2.jpg" height="197" width="613" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>11、组合模式（Composite）</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">组合模式有时又叫<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">部分-整体</span></strong>模式在处理类似树形结构的问题时比较方便，看看关系图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1205/09cab656-5ff9-380e-9df1-326339ac3509.jpg" height="177" width="483" alt=""></p>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">//取得孩子节点</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Enumeration&lt;TreeNode&gt;&nbsp;getChildren(){&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">return</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;children.elements();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Tree&nbsp;tree&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Tree(</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"A"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TreeNode&nbsp;nodeB&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;TreeNode(</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"B"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TreeNode&nbsp;nodeC&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;TreeNode(</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"C"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;nodeB.add(nodeC);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">使用场景：将多个对象组合在一起进行操作，常用于表示树形结构中，例如二叉树，数等。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>12、享元模式（Flyweight）</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">享元模式的主要目的是实现对象的共享，即共享池，当系统中对象多的时候可以减少内存的开销，通常与工厂模式一起使用。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1207/f7aae0dd-b250-3829-bb07-49d87069bfbb.jpg" height="171" width="484" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">FlyWeightFactory负责创建和管理享元单元，当一个客户端请求时，工厂需要检查当前对象池中是否有符合条件的对象，如果有，就返回已经存在的对象，如果没有，则创建一个新对象，FlyWeight是超类。一提到共享池，我们很容易联想到Java里面的JDBC连接池，想想每个连接的特点，我们不难总结出：适用于作共享的一些个对象，他们有一些共有的属性，就拿数据库连接池来说，url、driverClassName、username、password及dbname，这些属性对于每个连接来说都是一样的，所以就适合用享元模式来处理，建一个工厂类，将上述类似属性作为内部数据，其它的作为外部数据，在方法调用时，当做参数传进来，这样就节省了空间，减少了实例的数量。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">看个例子：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1209/53bc0bf4-cafb-3a12-8574-e20a525f2b72.jpg" height="196" width="452" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">看下数据库连接池的代码：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">

</div>

<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;ConnectionPool&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Vector&lt;Connection&gt;&nbsp;pool;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*公有属性*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;String&nbsp;url&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/test"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;String&nbsp;username&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"root"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;String&nbsp;password&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"root"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;String&nbsp;driverClassName&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"com.mysql.jdbc.Driver"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;poolSize&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">100</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">private</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;ConnectionPool&nbsp;instance&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">null</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Connection&nbsp;conn&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">null</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*&nbsp;返回连接池中的一个数据库连接&nbsp;*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">synchronized</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Connection&nbsp;getConnection()&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">if</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;(pool.size()&nbsp;&gt;&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">0</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Connection&nbsp;conn&nbsp;=&nbsp;pool.get(<span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">0</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;pool.remove(conn);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<div>&nbsp;</div>
<div>通过连接池的管理，实现了数据库连接的共享，不需要每一次都重新创建连接，节省了数据库重新创建的开销，提升了系统的性能！本章讲解了7种结构型模式，因为篇幅的问题，剩下的11种行为型模式，</div>
</div>
<div style="font-size: 14px;">
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">本章是关于设计模式的最后一讲，会讲到第三种设计模式——行为型模式，共11种：策略模式、模板方法模式、观察者模式、迭代子模式、责任链模式、命令模式、备忘录模式、状态模式、访问者模式、中介者模式、解释器模式。这段时间一直在写关于设计模式的东西，终于写到一半了，写博文是个很费时间的东西，因为我得为读者负责，不论是图还是代码还是表述，都希望能尽量写清楚，以便读者理解，我想不论是我还是读者，都希望看到高质量的博文出来，从我本人出发，我会一直坚持下去，不断更新，源源动力来自于读者朋友们的不断支持，我会尽自己的努力，写好每一篇文章！希望大家能不断给出意见和建议，共同打造完美的博文！</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><em><span style="font-size: 18px;"><strong>&nbsp;</strong></span></em></p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">先来张图，看看这11中模式的关系：</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">第一类：通过父类与子类的关系进行实现。第二类：两个类之间。第三类：类的状态。第四类：通过中间类</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1211/5e2feb58-4170-3c07-a370-ed99bdcab223.jpg" height="314" width="681" alt=""></p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>13、策略模式（strategy）</strong></span></p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">策略模式定义了一系列算法，并将每个算法封装起来，使他们可以相互替换，且算法的变化不会影响到使用算法的客户。需要设计一个接口，为一系列实现类提供统一的方法，多个实现类实现该接口，设计一个抽象类（可有可无，属于辅助类），提供辅助函数，关系图如下：</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1213/2319a2c3-7ebd-3ee3-b389-1548074ea9c6.jpg" height="260" width="560" alt=""></p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">图中ICalculator提供同意的方法，<br>AbstractCalculator是辅助类，提供辅助方法，接下来，依次实现下每个类：</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">首先统一接口：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">copy</a>
</div>

<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：10</p>
<p style="line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">策略模式的决定权在用户，系统本身提供不同算法的实现，新增或者删除算法，对各种算法做封装。因此，策略模式多用在算法决策系统中，外部用户只需要决定用哪个算法即可。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>14、模板方法模式（Template Method）</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">解释一下模板方法模式，就是指：一个抽象类中，有一个主方法，再定义1...n个方法，可以是抽象的，也可以是实际的方法，定义一个类，继承该抽象类，重写抽象方法，通过调用抽象类，实现对子类的调用，先看个关系图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1215/c3d57775-ddf9-302b-9dfe-c65967518d3c.jpg" height="205" width="478" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">就是在AbstractCalculator类中定义一个主方法calculate，calculate()调用spilt()等，Plus和Minus分别继承AbstractCalculator类，通过对AbstractCalculator的调用实现对子类的调用，看下面的例子：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">copy</a>
</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">abstract</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;AbstractCalculator&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*主方法，实现对本类其它方法的调用*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">final</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;calculate(String&nbsp;exp,String&nbsp;opt){&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;array[]&nbsp;=&nbsp;split(exp,opt);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">return</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;calculate(array[</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">0</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">],array[</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">1</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">]);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #008200; padding: 0px;">/*被子类重写的方法*/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">abstract</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;calculate(</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;num1,</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;num2);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">[]&nbsp;split(String&nbsp;exp,String&nbsp;opt){&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;String&nbsp;array[]&nbsp;=&nbsp;exp.split(opt);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;arrayInt[]&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">[</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">2</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">];&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;arrayInt[<span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">0</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">]&nbsp;=&nbsp;Integer.parseInt(array[</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">0</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">]);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;arrayInt[<span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">1</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">]&nbsp;=&nbsp;Integer.parseInt(array[</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #c00000; padding: 0px;">1</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">]);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>

<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">

<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">class</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;StrategyTest&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">static</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;main(String[]&nbsp;args)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;String&nbsp;exp&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"8+8"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;AbstractCalculator&nbsp;cal&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Plus();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">int</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;result&nbsp;=&nbsp;cal.calculate(exp,&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"\\+"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;System.out.println(result);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">我跟踪下这个小程序的执行过程：首先将exp和"\\+"做参数，调用AbstractCalculator类里的calculate(String,String)方法，在calculate(String,String)里调用同类的split()，之后再调用calculate(int ,int)方法，从这个方法进入到子类中，执行完return num1 + num2后，将值返回到AbstractCalculator类，赋给result，打印出来。正好验证了我们开头的思路。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>15、观察者模式（Observer）</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">包括这个模式在内的接下来的四个模式，都是类和类之间的关系，不涉及到继承，学的时候应该 记得归纳，记得本文最开始的那个图。观察者模式很好理解，类似于邮件订阅和RSS订阅，当我们浏览一些博客或wiki时，经常会看到RSS图标，就这的意思是，当你订阅了该文章，如果后续有更新，会及时通知你。其实，简单来讲就一句话：当一个对象变化时，其它依赖该对象的对象都会收到通知，并且随着变化！对象之间是一种一对多的关系。先来看看关系图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1233/d588525c-fbad-3040-971c-69b2716c67a4.jpg" height="380" width="626" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">我解释下这些类的作用：MySubject类就是我们的主对象，Observer1和Observer2是依赖于MySubject的对象，当MySubject变化时，Observer1和Observer2必然变化。AbstractSubject类中定义着需要监控的对象列表，可以对其进行修改：增加或删除被监控对象，且当MySubject变化时，负责通知在列表内存在的对象。我们看实现代码：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">一个Observer接口：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">copy</a>
</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">interface</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Observer&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;update();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">两个实现类：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">

<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">

<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">update self!<br>observer1 has received!<br>observer2 has received!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;这些东西，其实不难，只是有些抽象，不太容易整体理解，建议读者：<strong><span style="color: #333333; font-size: 12px;">根据关系图，新建项目，自己写代码（或者参考我的代码）,<strong>按照</strong>总体思路走一遍，这样才能体会它的思想，理解起来容易！</span></strong><strong style="color: #3333ff;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><strong><span style="color: #006600;">16、迭代子模式（Iterator）</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">顾名思义，迭代器模式就是顺序访问聚集中的对象，一般来说，集合中非常常见，如果对集合类比较熟悉的话，理解本模式会十分轻松。这句话包含两层意思：一是需要遍历的对象，即聚集对象，二是迭代器对象，用于对聚集对象进行遍历访问。我们看下关系图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;<img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1217/f7571a69-3c85-3fe1-b781-e460563a40a8.jpg" height="344" width="640" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">这个思路和我们常用的一模一样，MyCollection中定义了集合的一些操作，MyIterator中定义了一系列迭代操作，且持有Collection实例，我们来看看实现代码：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">两个接口：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">view plain</a><a title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/zhangerqing/article/details/8243942">copy</a>
</div>
</div>
<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">interface</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;Collection&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Collection&nbsp;collection&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;MyCollection();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Iterator&nbsp;it&nbsp;=&nbsp;collection.iterator();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">while</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">(it.hasNext()){&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;System.out.println(it.next());&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：A B C D E</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">此处我们貌似模拟了一个集合类的过程，感觉是不是很爽？其实JDK中各个类也都是这些基本的东西，加一些设计模式，再加一些优化放到一起的，只要我们把这些东西学会了，掌握好了，我们也可以写出自己的集合类，甚至框架！</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>17、责任链模式（Chain of Responsibility）<br></strong></span>接下来我们将要谈谈责任链模式，有多个对象，每个对象持有对下一个对象的引用，这样就会形成一条链，请求在这条链上传递，直到某一对象决定处理该请求。但是发出者并不清楚到底最终那个对象会处理该请求，所以，责任链模式可以实现，在隐瞒客户端的情况下，对系统进行动态的调整。先看看关系图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;<img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1219/729a82ce-0987-347c-a4f1-bf64dee59ddb.jpg" height="287" width="486" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">Abstracthandler类提供了get和set方法，方便MyHandle类设置和修改引用对象，MyHandle类是核心，实例化后生成一系列相互持有的对象，构成一条链。</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">public</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">void</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;operator()&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;MyHandler&nbsp;h2&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;MyHandler(</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"h2"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;MyHandler&nbsp;h3&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;MyHandler(</span><span style="margin: 0px; color: blue; padding: 0px;">"h3"</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;h1.setHandler(h2);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; background-color: #f8f8f8; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">输出：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">h1deal!<br>h2deal!<br>h3deal!</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">此处强调一点就是，链接上的请求可以是一条链，可以是一个树，还可以是一个环，模式本身不约束这个，需要我们自己去实现，同时，在一个时刻，命令只允许由一个对象传给另一个对象，而不允许传给多个对象。</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><span style="color: #006600;"><strong>&nbsp;18、命令模式（Command）</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">命令模式很好理解，举个例子，司令员下令让士兵去干件事情，从整个事情的角度来考虑，司令员的作用是，发出口令，口令经过传递，传到了士兵耳朵里，士兵去执行。这个过程好在，三者相互解耦，任何一方都不用去依赖其他人，只需要做好自己的事儿就行，司令员要的是结果，不会去关注到底士兵是怎么实现的。我们看看关系图：</p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://dl.iteye.com/upload/attachment/0083/1239/98cda4fc-00b1-300d-a25b-63229f0f1cbd.jpg" height="234" width="609" alt=""></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px; font-family: Arial; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px;">Invoker是调用者（司令员），Receiver是被调用者（士兵），MyCommand是命令，实现了Command接口，持有接收对象，看实现代码：</p>
<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">

<div style="text-align: left; line-height: 26px; background-color: #e7e5dc; margin: 18px 0px; width: 1314px; font-family: Consolas, 'Courier New', Courier, mono, serif; font-size: 12px; overflow: auto; padding-top: 1px;">
<div style="padding-left: 45px;">
<div style="border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 10px; line-height: normal; background-color: #f8f8f8; padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 8px; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: silver; font-size: 9px; padding-top: 3px;">

<ol style="background-color: #ffffff; margin: 0px 0px 1px 45px; color: #5c5c5c; padding: 0px;">

<li style="border-bottom-style: none; border-left: #6ce26c 3px solid; padding-bottom: 0px !important; line-height: 18px; border-right-style: none; margin: 0px; padding-left: 10px !important; padding-right: 3px !important; border-top-style: none; padding-top: 0px !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; color: black; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command&nbsp;cmd&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; color: #006699; font-weight: bold; padding: 0px;">new</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;MyCommand(receiver);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li>
